VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset seconds to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset minutes to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Reset hours to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Increment to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule
Compilation check...
Output Verilog module compiles successfully.

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(

    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,

VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Set to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Set to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

Output Verilog module compiles successfully.

    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Set to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Set to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset seconds to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset minutes to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Reset hours to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Increment to 12

                        minutes[7:4] <= minutes[7:4] + 1;
                    end
                end
            end

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Set to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Set to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 8'b0000_0001; // Increment hour
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 8'b0000_0001; // Increment minute
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 8'b0000_0001; // Increment second
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Set to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Set to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset seconds to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset minutes to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Reset hours to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Increment to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours[3:0] <= (hours[3:0] == 4'b1001) ? 4'b0000 : hours[3:0] + 1;
                        if (hours[3:0] == 4'b0000) begin
                            hours[7:4] <= hours[7:4] + 1;
                        end
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes[3:0] <= (minutes[3:0] == 4'b1001) ? 4'b0000 : minutes[3:0] + 1;
                    if (minutes[3:0] == 4'b0000) begin
                        minutes[7:4] <= minutes[7:4] + 1;
                    end
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds[3:0] <= (seconds[3:0] == 4'b1001) ? 4'b0000 : seconds[3:0] + 1;
                if (seconds[3:0] == 4'b0000) begin
                    seconds[7:4] <= seconds[7:4] + 1;
                end
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset seconds to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset minutes to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Reset hours to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Increment to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset seconds to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset minutes to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Reset hours to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Increment to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset seconds to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset minutes to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Reset hours to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Increment to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm; // 0 for AM, 1 for PM

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 1'b0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin
                seconds[3:0] <= 4'b0000;
                if (seconds[7:4] == 4'b0101) begin
                    seconds[7:4] <= 4'b0000;
                    
                    // Increment minutes
                    if (minutes[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin
                        minutes[3:0] <= 4'b0000;
                        if (minutes[7:4] == 4'b0101) begin
                            minutes[7:4] <= 4'b0000;
                            
                            // Increment hours
                            if (hours[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin
                                hours[3:0] <= 4'b0000;
                                if (hours[7:4] == 4'b0001) begin
                                    hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // 01 in BCD
                                    am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                                end
                                else begin
                                    hours[7:4] <= hours[7:4] + 1'b1;
                                end
                            end
                            else if (hours[3:0] == 4'b0010 && hours[7:4] == 4'b0001) begin
                                hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // 01 in BCD
                                am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                            end
                            else begin
                                hours[3:0] <= hours[3:0] + 1'b1;
                            end
                        end
                        else begin
                            minutes[7:4] <= minutes[7:4] + 1'b1;
                        end
                    end
                    else begin
                        minutes[3:0] <= minutes[3:0] + 1'b1;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    seconds[7:4] <= seconds[7:4] + 1'b1;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds[3:0] <= seconds[3:0] + 1'b1;
            end
        end
    end

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

endmodule

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset seconds to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset minutes to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Reset hours to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Increment to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 8'b0000_0001; // Increment hours
                    end
                end
                else if (minutes[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin
                    minutes <= {minutes[7:4] + 1'b1, 4'b0000}; // Increment tens place
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 8'b0000_0001; // Increment minutes
                end
            end
            else if (seconds[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin
                seconds <= {seconds[7:4] + 1'b1, 4'b0000}; // Increment tens place
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 8'b0000_0001; // Increment seconds
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

module top_module(

    input reset,

    assign ss = seconds;

    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Set to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Set to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Set to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Set to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset seconds to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset minutes to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Reset hours to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Increment to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 8'b0000_0001; // Increment hours
                    end
                end
                else if (minutes[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin
                    minutes <= {minutes[7:4] + 1'b1, 4'b0000}; // Increment tens place
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 8'b0000_0001; // Increment minutes
                end
            end
            else if (seconds[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin
                seconds <= {seconds[7:4] + 1'b1, 4'b0000}; // Increment tens place
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 8'b0000_0001; // Increment seconds
            end
        end
    end

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Set to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Set to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Set to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Set to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm; // 0 for AM, 1 for PM

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 1'b0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin
                seconds[3:0] <= 4'b0000;
                if (seconds[7:4] == 4'b0101) begin
                    seconds[7:4] <= 4'b0000;
                    
                    // Increment minutes
                    if (minutes[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin
                        minutes[3:0] <= 4'b0000;
                        if (minutes[7:4] == 4'b0101) begin
                            minutes[7:4] <= 4'b0000;
                            
                            // Increment hours
                            if (hours[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin
                                hours[3:0] <= 4'b0000;
                                if (hours[7:4] == 4'b0001) begin
                                    hours <= 8'b0001_0001; // 01 in BCD
                                    am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                                end
                                else begin
                                    hours[7:4] <= hours[7:4] + 1'b1;
                                end
                            end
                            else if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                                hours <= 8'b0001_0001; // 01 in BCD
                                am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                            end
                            else begin
                                hours[3:0] <= hours[3:0] + 1'b1;
                            end
                        end
                        else begin
                            minutes[7:4] <= minutes[7:4] + 1'b1;
                        end
                    end
                    else begin
                        minutes[3:0] <= minutes[3:0] + 1'b1;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    seconds[7:4] <= seconds[7:4] + 1'b1;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds[3:0] <= seconds[3:0] + 1'b1;
            end
        end
    end

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Set to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Set to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(

VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Set to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Set to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Set to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Set to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm; // 0 for AM, 1 for PM

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 1'b0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin
                seconds[3:0] <= 4'b0000;
                if (seconds[7:4] == 4'b0101) begin
                    seconds[7:4] <= 4'b0000;
                    
                    // Increment minutes
                    if (minutes[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin
                        minutes[3:0] <= 4'b0000;
                        if (minutes[7:4] == 4'b0101) begin
                            minutes[7:4] <= 4'b0000;
                            
                            // Increment hours
                            if (hours[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin
                                hours[3:0] <= 4'b0000;
                                if (hours[7:4] == 4'b0001) begin
                                    hours <= 8'b0001_0001; // 11 in BCD
                                end else begin
                                    hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
                                    am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                                end
                            end else if ((hours == 8'b0001_0010) && (hours[3:0] == 4'b0010)) begin
                                hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // 01 in BCD
                            end else begin
                                hours[3:0] <= hours[3:0] + 1'b1;
                            end
                        end else begin
                            minutes[7:4] <= minutes[7:4] + 1'b1;
                        end
                    end else begin
                        minutes[3:0] <= minutes[3:0] + 1'b1;
                    end
                end else begin
                    seconds[7:4] <= seconds[7:4] + 1'b1;
                end
            end else begin
                seconds[3:0] <= seconds[3:0] + 1'b1;
            end
        end
    end

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;
endmodule

VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Set to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0000_1001) begin // 09 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0000; // Set to 10
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0000) begin // 10 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0001; // Set to 11
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Set to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset seconds to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset minutes to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Reset hours to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Increment to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,

    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);


API response time: 5.032465 seconds
trimming code...
Initiating comile/functionality check.
VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Set to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Set to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(

    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,

    output [7:0] ss);

    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

        if (reset) begin

            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end

                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD

                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Reset hours to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Increment to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Set to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Set to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset seconds to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset minutes to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Reset hours to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Increment to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours[3:0] <= (hours[3:0] == 4'b1001) ? 4'b0000 : hours[3:0] + 1;
                        if (hours[3:0] == 4'b0000) begin
                            hours[7:4] <= hours[7:4] + 1;
                        end
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes[3:0] <= (minutes[3:0] == 4'b1001) ? 4'b0000 : minutes[3:0] + 1;
                    if (minutes[3:0] == 4'b0000) begin
                        minutes[7:4] <= minutes[7:4] + 1;
                    end
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds[3:0] <= (seconds[3:0] == 4'b1001) ? 4'b0000 : seconds[3:0] + 1;
                if (seconds[3:0] == 4'b0000) begin
                    seconds[7:4] <= seconds[7:4] + 1;
                end
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Set to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Set to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Set to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Set to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours[3:0] <= hours[3:0] + 1'b1;
                    end
                end
                else if (minutes[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin // 9 in BCD
                    minutes[3:0] <= 4'b0000;
                    minutes[7:4] <= minutes[7:4] + 1'b1;
                end
                else begin
                    minutes[3:0] <= minutes[3:0] + 1'b1;
                end
            end
            else if (seconds[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin // 9 in BCD
                seconds[3:0] <= 4'b0000;
                seconds[7:4] <= seconds[7:4] + 1'b1;
            end
            else begin
                seconds[3:0] <= seconds[3:0] + 1'b1;
            end
        end
    end

endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end

            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset seconds to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset minutes to 00
                    // Increment hours

                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Reset hours to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM

                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Increment to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end
                else begin

                end
            end
